That is why the Wordfence Intelligence [user interface](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/threat-intel\/>), [vulnerability API](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/help\/wordfence-intelligence\/v2-accessing-and-consuming-the-vulnerability-data-feed\/>), [webhook integration](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/help\/wordfence-intelligence-webhook-notifications\/>), and [Wordfence CLI Vulnerability Scanner](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-cli\/>) are all completely free to access and utilize both personally and commercially, and why we are running this weekly vulnerability report.\n\nEnterprises, Hosting Providers, and even Individuals can use the [Wordfence CLI Vulnerability Scanner](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-cli\/>) to run regular vulnerability scans across the sites they protect. Or alternatively, utilize the [vulnerability Database API](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/help\/wordfence-intelligence\/v2-accessing-and-consuming-the-vulnerability-data-feed\/>) to receive a complete dump of our database of over 15,000 vulnerabilities and then utilize the [webhook integration](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/help\/wordfence-intelligence-webhook-notifications\/>) to stay on top of the newest vulnerabilities added in real-time, as well as any updates made to the database, **all for free**.\n\n_[Click here to sign-up for our mailing list](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/subscribe-to-the-wordfence-email-list\/>) to receive weekly vulnerability reports like this and important WordPress Security reports in your inbox the moment they are published._\n\n* * *\n\n### New Firewall Rules Deployed Last Week\n\nThe Wordfence Threat Intelligence Team reviews each vulnerability to determine impact and severity, along with assessing the likelihood of exploitation, to verify that the Wordfence Firewall provides sufficient protection.\n\nThe team rolled out enhanced protection via firewall rules for the following vulnerabilities in real-time to our [Premium](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-premium\/>), [Care](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-care\/>), and [Response](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-response\/>) customers last week:\n\n  * WAF-RULE-685 \u2013 Data redacted while we work with the vendor on a patch.\n  * WAF-RULE-687 \u2013 Data redacted while we work with the vendor on a patch.\n\nWordfence [Premium](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-premium\/>), [Care](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-care\/>), and [Response](<https:\/\/www.wordfence.com\/products\/wordfence-response\/>) customers received this protection immediately, while users still running the free version of Wordfence will receive this enhanced protection after a 30 day delay.\n\n* * *\n\n### Total Unpatched &amp; Patched Vulnerabilities Last Week\n\nPatch Status |
